[?2004l[?1049h[22;0;0t[?1h=SCRIPT(1)                        User Commands                       SCRIPT(1)[m
[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       script - make typescript of terminal session[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mscript[0m [options] [[4mfile[24m][m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       [1mscript[0m makes a typescript of everything on your terminal session. The[m
       terminal data are stored in raw form to the log file and information[m
       about timing to another (optional) structured log file. The timing log[m
       file is necessary to replay the session later by [1mscriptreplay[0m(1) and to[m
       store additional information about the session.[m
[m
       Since version 2.35, [1mscript[0m supports multiple streams and allows the[m
       logging of input and output to separate files or all the one file. This[m
       version also supports new timing file which records additional[m
       information. The command [1mscriptreplay[0m [1m--summary[0m then provides all the[m
       information.[m
[m
       If the argument [4mfile[24m or option [1m--log-out[0m [4mfile[24m is given, [1mscript[0m saves[m
       the dialogue in this [4mfile[24m. If no filename is given, the dialogue is[m
[7m Manual page script(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K[?1l>[?1049l[23;0;0tNo manual entry for gdbdebug.txt
